 Emoji Keyboard/Display Test Data for UTS 51
 Version 15.0

 For docutation and usage see https//www.unicode.org/reports/tr51

 This file provides data for testing which emoji forms should be in keyboards and which should also be displayed/processed.
 Format code points status  emoji name
     Code points â€” list of one or more hex code points separated by spaces
     Status
       component           â€” an Emoji_Component
                             excluding Regional_Indicators ASCII and nonEmoji.
            â€” a  emoji (see ED18 in UTS 51)
                             excluding Emoji_Component
        â€” a  emoji (see ED18a in UTS 51)
                â€” a  emoji (See ED19 in UTS 51)
 Notes
   â€¢ This includes the emoji components that need emoji presentation (  and hair)
     when isolated but omits the components that need not have an emoji
     presentation when isolated.
   â€¢ The RGI set is covered by the listed  emoji. 
   â€¢ The listed  and  cover all cases where an
     elet of the RGI set is missing one or more emoji presentation selectors.
   â€¢ The file is in CLDR order not codepoint order. This is recomded (but not required!) for keyboard palettes.
   â€¢ The groups and subgroups are illustrative. See the Emoji Order chart for more information.
